China Merchants Bureau Appoints Senior Officials; Existing Employees to Undergo Screening 122

Cai Zengji, the general manager of the state-owned China Merchants Bureau, and the two deputy general managers, Tan Boying and Lao Mian, were sworn into office the day before yesterday morning. Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Further news obtained yesterday is reported below.

Qualifications of New Employees

The organization of the bureau, which has been approved and revised by the Ministry of Transportation, only has two secretaries. Yesterday, Cai appointed Ma Shaohuai and Chen Guoquan to fill the roles. Ma served as the secretary director of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau for many years. Chen is an accounting expert and served as the bureau's chief auditor when Guo Waifeng was a commissioner of the China Merchants Bureau, so he is very familiar with the bureau's affairs. Furthermore, Chen Weiqing, the director of the bureau's General Affairs Department, resigned, and Cai appointed Wang Xiangchen as acting director yesterday. The deputy director position in that department remains vacant, and Chen Bingchi was appointed as acting deputy director. Wang previously served as the head of the second and third sections of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau, assisting Cai in handling municipal government bond affairs with great success. Chen accompanied Cai when he represented the Ministry of Railways in inspecting European and American railway administration and studying the reorganization of railway debt, serving as chief secretary. He is also well-versed in debt reorganization. Cai, realizing that the China Merchants Bureau's debt urgently needs reorganization, invited Wang and Chen to take on the positions in the General Affairs Department to assist him. As for the original directors and deputy directors of the Business Department, they have already resigned. Currently, Deputy General Manager Tan is temporarily serving as acting director, and Zhou Fengtu, the former joint transportation commissioner, has been transferred to serve as acting deputy director. Zhou has worked in the bureau for many years and has studied maritime and land transportation abroad, earning a doctoral degree. Cai specially invited him to assist. Furthermore, the original director of the Shipping Department resigned, and Cai has transferred Teng Shibiao, captain of the Haili ship, to serve as acting director. Because the newly reorganized bureau has eliminated the originally established position of chief shipmaster, the director of the Shipping Department should be someone who is familiar with driving personnel. Moreover, the Haili ship is one of the bureau's four new ships, and its operation has been the most successful and economical. Therefore, Captain Teng was transferred to the bureau to oversee the department. Before Teng arrives, Deputy Director Zhou Houkun will temporarily serve as acting director. It is said that Cai adheres to the principle of talent when hiring people, so the above-mentioned positions have all been filled by qualified personnel. In addition, Cai Zhongming was appointed as the director of the Treasury, and Luo Hai was appointed as the seal supervisor. Furthermore, the manager of the Suzhou Inland River Shipping Bureau resigned, and Deputy Manager Lao Mian is currently serving as acting manager.

Screening to be Conducted Immediately

The screening of bureau employees is already actively underway. Yesterday, the Secretariat issued the first notice, stating roughly, "By order of the General Manager, each department head is required to submit a detailed report on the work abilities of all employees under their jurisdiction within fifteen days." Subsequently, the second notice was issued, stating, "By order of the General Manager, all bureau employees are required to submit a detailed report on their resumes and handled duties within two days, along with a two-inch photograph, for review." Each department head and employee is complying with the notice. This is because, before the examination is held, the work experience of each employee must first be reviewed to determine eligibility.

Bureau Director Hopes to Waive Exam

The China Merchants Bureau employees have an organization called the Public Welfare Association, with a total of 195 members. The day before yesterday, upon hearing about the reorganization, they submitted a petition to the General Manager requesting that the examination system be waived. They received a reply that they still had to follow the ministry's order. Yesterday, the association sent seven representatives to meet with General Manager Cai to congratulate him on his inauguration and to inquire about Cai's plan to retain 60 to 70 employees in accordance with the ministry's order, which they believed was sufficient to manage the overall affairs. At that time, Cai said that the number of employees was determined by the ministry and that he would only follow the order. As for the examination, it was also necessary to conduct screening in accordance with the ministry's order, and it was not possible to waive the exam.

Gu Zhuxuan Case Not Pronounced Yesterday 126

Debate Concluded Yesterday, Rescheduled for Retrial; Due to New Facts Emerging, Investigation Underway

Gu Zhuxuan of Yancheng, the former owner of the Tianchan Stage, and Wang Xinggao of Funing were involved in the assassination of Tang Jiapeng, the former manager of the Great World Amusement Park, and were implicated in the crime of instigating the assassination. The French Concession Police arrested Wang and Gu one after another and transferred them to the Special Second Court. Gu was sentenced to fifteen years in prison, and Wang was sentenced to life imprisonment. Dissatisfied, they filed appeals with the Higher Third Branch Court. On the 4th of this month, the Higher Third Branch Court opened a collegial panel to hear both cases on the same day, one in the morning and one in the afternoon, and announced the conclusion of the debate, scheduling the pronouncement of the verdict for 2:00 PM yesterday. During this period, new complications suddenly arose in both cases. The Higher Third Branch Court noticed this and sent personnel to conduct a secret investigation. Due to the seriousness of the circumstances, the three prison guards who were at large were ordered to be detained, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, when the time for the pronouncement of the verdict in both cases arrived, the French Concession Police Department dispatched a reserve team and detectives as before to protect the area around the court. Another group of detectives, together with court police officers, maintained order in the First Court. The audience was also very crowded. When the clock struck two, Chinese and French police officers and French Concession detectives, together with the head of the detention center, went to Guangci Hospital to bring Gu Zhuxuan to the waiting room behind the First Court for temporary detention. Then, they went to the detention center to bring Wang Xinggao up and temporarily detain him in the waiting room upstairs. At 2:25 PM, Sun Honglin, the acting presiding judge of the Higher Third Branch Court, accompanied by Wang Yue and Li Changnian, judges, and Wu Jiayu, clerk, along with Chief Prosecutor Zhao Shibei, arrived at Criminal Court No. 1. Lawyer Yao Zhaodi represented the French Concession Police Department in court. On the appellant side, only Wang Xinggao's defense lawyer, Wu Gonglun, was present. First, Wang Xinggao was brought to the case, and after a brief inquiry into his age and origin, Judge Sun announced that after the conclusion of the debate in your case, the court discovered a new fact related to your case. After a thorough investigation, another hearing will be scheduled. Today, the conclusion of the debate is revoked, and no verdict will be pronounced. Wang nodded upon hearing the announcement and remained silent. The official ordered Wang to be taken back into custody. Then, Gu Zhuxuan was brought to the case, and after a brief inquiry into his age and origin, Judge Sun announced to Gu, "Your case was originally scheduled to be pronounced today. However, after the court announced the conclusion of the debate, a new fact emerged. After a thorough investigation, the debate will be reopened. No verdict will be pronounced today, and the conclusion of the debate is revoked. A retrial will be scheduled after the investigation." Gu asked the court what the new fact was. The official announced that he would be notified when the retrial was scheduled, and there was no need to say more today. After the announcement, he ordered Gu to be taken back into custody and declared the court adjourned.

Famous Actress Anna May Wong Enters the Country for the First Time Yesterday 127

Plans to Stay in Shanghai for Two Weeks, Then Go to Her Ancestral Home in Taishan, Guangdong

According to the Central News Agency, Anna May Wong, the famous Chinese-American film actress who has dedicated herself to the silver screen in the United States for fifteen years, was born and raised in California and has never set foot in her ancestral homeland. After returning to the United States from a tour of Europe last year, she suddenly felt homesick and decided to return to China for the first time. She plans to travel to major cities throughout the country, such as Shanghai, Nanjing, Beijing, Hankou, and Guangzhou, in order to correct her past mistakes of playing roles in some films that misrepresented the true lives of Chinese women, due to her lack of understanding. She hopes that after returning to Hollywood, she can use her current position to reintroduce Chinese women to film audiences around the world. Wong arrived in Shanghai from the United States yesterday aboard the Dollar Steamship Lines' President Hoover. Wong's only relative in Shanghai is her elder brother, Wong Jinshu, who has a master's degree in business from the University of Southern California. He also decided to come to Shanghai two months ago. Therefore, at 3:00 PM yesterday, only her brother and two female friends she met in England and the United States went to the New Customs Wharf on a small Dollar Steamship Lines boat to welcome her. Wong wore a black long-sleeved Western suit, black stockings, and black shoes, and a specially made black cat-shaped felt hat. She met with the welcomers and Chinese and foreign journalists in the ship's reception room. Wong, who is thirty years old, is tall and healthy, and her face appears slightly aged, but her social demeanor and light makeup still remind people of her alluring beauty from her days with Douglas Fairbanks in "The Thief of Bagdad." It has not been that long since then. She first posed for photos with reporters on the deck and spoke to reporters in fluent English about her personal life, her thoughts on her film career, and her travel plans. Then, she went down to the small boat with her brother and female friends and arrived at the New Customs Wharf at 4:20 PM. After inspecting her luggage, she was advised by a French police officer to avoid the crowds in front and take the south iron gate. However, she was still surrounded by the crowd, so she seized the opportunity to enter the customs house from the main entrance across the road and took car number 4481 to the International Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road, checking into room 1201. That evening, she went to the Grovano Building on Medhurst Road for a welcome dinner hosted by Wellington Koo's sister-in-law. The United Film Corporation will also hold a large banquet to welcome this returning film star. Wong plans to stay in Shanghai for two weeks, then return to her ancestral home in Taishan, Guangdong, to visit her 72-year-old father. She may also visit Java and Bali before returning north to visit Beijing, Tianjin, Pinghan, and other places. Then, she will return to Shanghai and go to Hollywood to continue her work. Wong studied Chinese for four years and can read newspapers, but she can only speak Cantonese, which is not very fluent. She has recently paid attention to national affairs and often refuses to act in films that insult China. This return to China will surely provide her with many lessons. Her recent work was the British Gaumont Film Company's "Java Head," which was completed last year.

General Manager of American Oriental Banking Corporation, German Gräupner, Accused 128

The victims are Chinese Yang Xiqing and Russian Iput De. The money they deposited with the bank was altered to call deposits without authorization. -- Gräupner is accused of embezzlement, fraud, and breach of trust --

The American Oriental Banking Corporation closed on May 24th of last year. The American Eastern Banking Corporation, Pu Yi Trust Company, and Pu Yi Real Estate Company, which were related to the bank, were also affected and subsequently went bankrupt. After the U.S. Consular Court in Shanghai dispatched personnel to investigate, it was discovered that the bank's chairman, American Raven, and key officer Bai Lang, had engaged in embezzlement, fraud, and breach of trust. The investigator then filed a lawsuit with the U.S. Consular Court against Raven and Bai Lang. Recently, Raven was sentenced to five years in prison and Bai Lang to two years. After Raven was convicted, he reportedly considered appealing, while Bai Lang admitted his guilt and indicated his willingness to forgo an appeal and enter prison.

Deserved Punishment

He has indicated that he will forego the appeal and is willing to enter prison and experience prison life. However, besides the evidence of malfeasance by Raven and Bai Lang uncovered by the investigator, Suzhou resident Yang Xiqing, who traded in gold, deposited 20,000 yuan in cash with the bank for safekeeping on April 8th of last year. After the bank closed, it was discovered that the deposit had been changed to a call deposit, preventing Yang from retrieving his money to this day. Someone named Iput De suffered the same loss as Yang. On April 30th of last year, Mr. Iput De also deposited 12,000 yuan with the bank for safekeeping, which was also changed to a

Call Deposit

Since the U.S. Consular Court has no jurisdiction over Yang and Iput De, and Gräupner, the vice-chairman and general manager of American Oriental Banking Corporation who is alleged to be responsible for these two incidents, is of German nationality, the court notified the Public Concession Police to investigate according to the law. Lawyer Ru Bao Yi of the police bureau's legal department then filed a public prosecution with the First Special District Court against Gräupner for embezzlement, fraud, and breach of trust. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qian Hongye opened the court to hear the case. The defendant appeared with his defense lawyer Chen Tingrui and a foreigner. Lawyer Chen stated that Gräupner is currently

Suffering from Heart Disease

He is particularly attending the court today despite his sickness and asked the court to allow him to sit down while waiting for the trial. The court permitted it. Then lawyer Ru Bao Yi stated the intention of the prosecution, essentially saying that the defendant Gräupner, as the vice-chairman and general manager, was fully responsible for the American Oriental Banking Corporation. His deputy manager was the nephew of Raven, who has already been sentenced to five years in prison, also named Raven. The first victim in this case, Yang Xiqing, was originally friendly with the bank's compradore Wang Yisui. On April 8th of last year, Yang took 20,000 yuan in cash to American Oriental Banking Corporation to visit Wang and asked him to

Exchange the Cash

And give the cash to the American Oriental Banking Corporation for safekeeping. Wang then consulted the defendant, who instructed Wang to tell Yang to make it a "call deposit." The nature of this type of deposit is that it requires prior notification before maturity and payment on the due date. However, Yang did not agree with the defendant's intention as relayed by Wang. Wang then discussed it with the defendant again. As a result, Wang accepted Yang's money according to the defendant's instructions and said that the safekeeping procedures would be followed, giving Yang a safekeeping receipt for 20,000 yuan and having Yang sign and leave a seal at the bank for verification when withdrawing the money in the future. The receipt was signed by Zhu Yousong, the director of the vault, and Deputy Manager Raven. In reality, the 20,000 yuan

Was Not Stored in the Vault

But Zhu and Raven signed on the receipt under the defendant's order. Although the bank's safekeeping ledger had a record of Yang's 20,000 yuan deposit, it noted beside it that it was a call deposit. To further make up for the lack of procedures, in addition to the safekeeping receipt given to Yang, another "call deposit" receipt was created and stored in the vault to comply with the rules. This shows that it was not an accidental error, but a planned act. Therefore, no one knew at first. When the bank closed, Yang asked the investigator, Hof, to return the money, but the vault was found to be

Completely Empty

With only the "call deposit" receipt remaining. The matter was then exposed. The first victim, Iput De, has already left Shanghai. His loss was 12,000 yuan, and the circumstances of his loss were roughly the same as Yang's. The difference is that Iput De originally had money deposited in American Oriental Banking Corporation. On April 30th of last year, he instructed the bank to withdraw part of the deposit and convert it to safekeeping. Therefore, he also held a safekeeping receipt, etc. The court then questioned Yang Xiqing about the facts of the matter. Yang described the entire process in detail and stated that he had always been in contact with Wang Yisui and had not directly met with the defendant. Wang Yisui, the witness, was then called to testify, stating that Yang had

Twenty Thousand Yuan in Cash

To exchange for cash and deposit it with American Oriental Banking Corporation. At the time, I asked the defendant, who asked me what Yang wanted to do with it. I told the defendant that Yang was worried that the banknotes might not be cashed in the future, so he took this action. The defendant then told me to have Yang change it to a call deposit, but Yang was unwilling. The defendant then ordered me to accept Yang's money and give him a safekeeping receipt. The banknotes were then deposited into the Bank of China by me on the same day, credited to American Oriental Banking Corporation’s account. It was not until American Oriental Banking Corporation closed that I learned that only a call deposit receipt was stored in the vault. As the bank's compradore, I was under a

Contractual Relationship

With the defendant, and should obey him absolutely, etc. Next, Zhu Yousong, the director of the vault, testified that all the procedures for changing the safekeeping deposits of Yang and Iput De to call deposits were carried out under the orders of the defendant. The court then questioned the defendant Gräupner, who stated that when cash is deposited with the bank for safekeeping, the bank should not move the money. The nature of safekeeping is different from the nature of deposit. Yang Xiqing deposited money with American Oriental Banking Corporation for safekeeping, and the receipt given was also a safekeeping receipt. How it later became a

Deposit Receipt

Is unclear. This is Zhu Yousong's responsibility. I usually focus on foreign exchange matters and rarely ask about ordinary matters. I don't understand what Wang and Zhu said because I don't know Chinese. The court then roughly told him the general meaning of what Wang and Zhu said. The defendant continued, stating that if I had ordered them to do so, there would have to be written proof, etc. Lawyer Chen then said that the content of this case is extremely complicated and cannot be clarified with a few words. The defendant intends to prepare a defense and requests additional witnesses to be summoned to clarify the truth. Therefore, he requests a postponement. Judge Qian then ordered the defendant to post a bail of 20,000 yuan and rescheduled the hearing for Thursday afternoon.

Celebrities from All Walks of Life Publicly Celebrate Cai Yuanpei's Seventieth Birthday 129

Mr. Cai's aesthetic education research institute was launched on the spot. Shen Enfu, Liu Yazi and others improvised poems.

The Shanghai Art College, China Vocational Education Society, Hongying Education Foundation Committee, China Art Education Society, and other cultural groups, Sun Ke, Kong Yongzhi, Wu Tiecheng, Qian Yongming, Liu Haisu, Shen Enfu, and others, initiated a public celebration of Cai Yuanpei's seventieth birthday at the International Hotel yesterday. Over one hundred and seventy celebrities from party, government, academic circles attended, including Sun Ke, He Yingqin, Zhang Xueliang, Gu Shaochuan, Wu Tiecheng, Liu Yazi, Du Yuesheng, Mei Lanfang, Li Denghui, etc. The traffic on Jing'an Temple Road was heavy, making it a grand occasion. Qian Xinzhi, Liu Haisu, Yan Kechang, and others were responsible for receiving the guests. At 7:00 p.m., Liu Hairuo, a member of the preparatory committee, went to Cai's residence to respectfully welcome Mr. Cai and his wife to the venue. Everyone stood up and applauded thunderously, creating a festive atmosphere. The banquet began at 7:30 p.m., chaired by Liu Haisu. President Sun Ke was invited to deliver a congratulatory speech on behalf of the attendees.

Sun's Congratulatory Speech

Today, we are holding this grand banquet to celebrate Mr. Cai's birthday. Mr. Cai's morality and learning are admired by the world. His contributions to society and the country have been profound and significant. Everyone here has a deep understanding of this, so I don't need to say more. There are two important meanings to our gathering today to celebrate Mr. Cai's seventieth birthday: We often say that it is rare for people to live to seventy years old since ancient times. Mr. Cai is now seventy years old and still in good health, which is cause for celebration among colleagues. Mr. Cai is not only a veteran of the party and country, but also a leading figure in the academic world of our country, admired by all. Therefore, we hope that Mr. Cai's spirit will continue to be healthy and continue to benefit society and the country. We will hold even grander celebrations when Mr. Cai is eighty, ninety, or even one hundred years old. In addition to celebrating Mr. Cai, we should also learn from Mr. Cai's past efforts for the country and society. We hope that everyone present can have Mr. Cai's longevity to shoulder the great difficulties of the future and build a country that can last forever. This is the meaning of our celebration today. I am participating in this celebration banquet today, and I will only say a few words. Please stand up and give Mr. Cai a salute. Cai then replied.

Cai's Response

Today, I am honored to have friends from the political, business, and academic circles celebrate my birthday, which I am truly unworthy of. There are many people in the party, country, and academic circles who are older than me and have more blessings, longevity, and sons. Therefore, my age cannot be considered very high. Nowadays, many people study the art of rejuvenation. Our country has also had it for a long time. Doctors such as those in the late Tang Dynasty involved the saying of immortals. Emperor Qin Shi Huang asked magicians to sail to the East China Sea to seek the elixir of immortality. Emperor Wu of Han also sought the method of immortality. This is because they had many achievements that they could not give up. However, Wu Meicun, a poet of the early Qing Dynasty, submitted to the court and later wrote many wonderful poems full of sorrow and chaos, "This disease is difficult to cure with medicine, and the hot blood in my heart" is his pain of losing the country. But if he had died ten years earlier, he would not have witnessed this heartache. The ancients said that being old and not dying is a thief. We are now at the same juncture, and there is a sense of great difficulty coming. Some people who live a few more years can still benefit the country and society, which is not without merit. Today, you are here to celebrate my birthday, and Mr. Sun's words just now are nothing more than wanting me to do a few more years of work. I am very ashamed. The ancients knew the mistakes of the past forty-nine years when they were fifty years old. I am now seventy, and there are twenty more years of mistakes. Living a few more years is nothing more than asking me to do a few more years of wrong things. As a writer, I can only do some work with my pen. In the past, every time I met Mr. Hu Shi, he always encouraged me to write an autobiography. I also wanted to use my remaining years to write something to thank society. Today, the chairmen, everyone and I wish me birthday, and I will never forget the meaning of wanting me to do my best for society and the country.

Founding of the Research Institute

During the banquet, Mayor Wu and others proposed to establish a cultural organization to commemorate Mr. Cai, because Mr. Cai has devoted himself to cultural education and art for decades, sparing no effort. Cai expressed his willingness to focus on aesthetic education in his speech, so it was unanimously decided to launch the Zimin Aesthetic Education Research Institute as a permanent memorial. Sun Ke, Kong Yongzhi, Liu Yazi, Huang Boqiao, Wang Xiaolai, Wu Tiecheng, Qian Xinzhi, Wang Yunwu, Liu Haisu, Pan Gongzhan, Li Dachao, and others were nominated as preparatory members, with President Sun and Mayor Wu as conveners. The banquet was filled with toasts and cheers. At 10:00 p.m., the banquet ended. President Sun immediately inscribed the four characters "Old and Strong," which Mr. Cai accepted with a smile. Wang Yiting, Yan Ganyuan, and Liu Haisu immediately painted multiple paintings of pine and cypress as birthday gifts. Shen Enfu immediately wrote a poem saying, "Occasionally I remember Confucius writing his autobiography, in that year at seventy his conduct followed his heart's desire. How much more should we respect you, Mr. Cai, as an elder statesman of the new nation, forever a teacher and admired by the scholars." Liu Yazi immediately wrote a poem, "In this era, your reputation surpasses all others, and future evaluations will surpass Confucius. I admire Lin Gengbai's saying that even the unyielding Han Yu would bow his head." For the celebration, the hosts and guests were in high spirits until 11:00 p.m.

Two Detectives Acquitted in Case of Killing a Chinese Man 131

Peter, a Western detective, and Jute, a probationary detective, from the Jiaxing Road Police Station, were accused of intentionally killing Chinese citizen Ma Debiao. The case was heard in the British Court for China yesterday morning. The defendants, Peter and Jute, were brought to court. Chief Judge Moss gave a detailed account of the case and the process of repeated trials to the jurors. After the statement, the jurors retired to the room to deliberate on whether the two defendants were guilty. After 42 minutes, the jurors returned to the court and deemed the two defendants not guilty. Chief Judge Moss then declared the two defendants not guilty.

Interesting Incident of Lawyer Jin Yu Encountering a Pickpocket 132

One Hundred and Fifty Yuan Vanishes Unexpectedly, Contracts, Seals, Etc. Returned Intact

Local Shanghai lawyer Jin Yu, whose courtesy name is Liren, has been practicing law in Shanghai for many years. His law firm is located at No. 68 Ningbo Road in the French Concession. However, Jin is tall and stout, with a large belly. At first glance, one would suspect him to be a tout, and would never think that he is a lawyer. Jin is fond of Zhou operas. Whenever he is free from work, he often accompanies his family to major theaters to enjoy the Peking operas performed by famous actors. The night before last, he accompanied his wife to the Xinguang Grand Theater on Tianjin Road to watch the full performance of "One Scoop of Snow" by famous actors Ma Lianliang, Hua Huilin, and Ye Sheng. By the time the performance ended, it was past 1 a.m. yesterday morning. At that time, Jin followed the audience out in single file. Just as he reached the exit of the gate and stopped to look around for his car, several well-dressed people resembling formal businessmen suddenly pushed past Jin. At this time, Jin suddenly felt a strange movement on the steel chain attached to his wallet in his pocket. He quickly reached into his pocket, but the wallet had disappeared. The steel chain had been cut into two pieces. Jin, who is experienced in Shanghai and naturally quick-witted, immediately turned around and grabbed one of the people who had pushed past him. Unexpectedly, this person began to speak in a heavy Beijing accent, repeatedly asking, "What are you doing?" Jin sternly ordered him to "be sensible" and dragged him into the car. At this time, the man asked Jin to go to a certain hotel first, promising to compensate him in full. Jin said that there was a total of 150 yuan in French currency in the wallet, and most importantly, it contained important contracts entrusted by the client, worth more than 60,000 yuan. In any case, they must be returned immediately, or he would go to the police station. The man asked Jin to wait a moment and immediately called his companions. Unexpectedly, the reply said that the French currency in the wallet had already been spent (meaning that they had already divided the spoils), and the people had already dispersed. Mr. Jin's wallet and the contracts and seals in the wallet had already been sent directly to Mr. Jin's law firm. Please return home to check and receive them to avoid loss in transit. As for the 150 yuan in French currency, it will be fully returned in a few days, and we will never break our promise. The man told Jin this. Jin was still half-believing, because Jin knew very well that there were no business cards or addresses in the wallet. How could they know so quickly, even if they sent someone to inquire about the address? He firmly refused. At this time, the man discussed with Jin, intending to have someone guarantee it. Jin heard that he knew that person, so he agreed. Soon, that person arrived and promised to return 150 yuan in full in the near future. After speaking, Jin hurried back to his residence by car. First, he searched downstairs, but there was no sign of the wallet. When he went upstairs to check, the items lost at the entrance of Xinguang had already been found on the balcony upstairs in Jin's lawyer's residence. After checking the items, everything was there except for the 150 yuan in French currency. At this time, lawyer Jin deeply sighed at the magical skills of the thieves and admired their superb thieving techniques. Yesterday, he specially told people to pay attention.

Shen Xin's Factories' Business Status Last Year 133

All Factories Have Surplus, Three Factories Are the Best

Rong Zongjing founded the Shen Xin Textile Company, which has as many as nine factories. Although there was a twist in the road the year before last, fortunately, with the strong maintenance of the party and government authorities, it was able to safely survive the difficulties. Last year, all factories were able to engage in technological and management improvements. Therefore, except for the two factories, No. 2 and No. 5, which did not start construction, the other factories have also made special progress compared to the old days. Shen Xin No. 3 Factory in Wuxi and Shen Xin No. 4 Factory in Hankou are earnestly focusing on the training of labor technology education, so the progress is very rapid. The cost per piece of yarn has reached above the horizontal level. Last year, the turnover of each factory was: the first factory had a surplus of more than 100,000 yuan, the third factory had a surplus of more than 200,000 yuan, the fourth factory had a surplus of 80,000 yuan, the sixth and seventh factories had not much up and down, and the ninth factory also had a slight surplus. It is also heard that Rong's Maoxin, Fuxin, and other flour mills, of which there are more than twelve, were also diligently managed by the managers hired by Rong, such as Wang, Lu, and Zhang. The profits of each factory are several times higher than that of the spinning mills. A reporter from Xinxinshe met Rong on the road yesterday and had a brief conversation. I felt that Rong's ambition to run real estate was no less than in the past, and his spirit and courage were better than in the past. He told me that he should devote himself to the improvement of the yarn and flour industry in the future in order to achieve the revitalization of the national industry.

Municipal Zoo Will Have Bears on Display 135

Gifted by Ueno Zoo in Tokyo, the zoo returned a male fish-scaled peacock. Shen Xiangrui is scheduled to leave Japan and return to China in mid-April.

Xu Bingrong, acting director of the Municipal Zoo on Wenmiao Road, received a letter from Mr. Shen Xiangrui, director of the zoo, from Japan, saying that a bear had recently been donated by Ueno Imperial Zoo in Japan and could be shipped to Shanghai for display. The details are as follows:

Scheduled to Return to China

Shen Xiangrui, director of the Municipal Zoo on Wenmiao Road, was sent to Ueno Imperial Zoo in Tokyo, Japan, in October last year to study animal administration and animal disease prevention. Now that he has completed his studies, he is scheduled to travel to various ports in Japan at the beginning of next month to continue inspecting the livestock industry and social education, etc., for a period of one month. He is scheduled to return to China in mid-April.

Donation of a Bear

Mr. Koga, director of Ueno Imperial Zoo, in order to maintain good relations as Shen was about to leave, specially presented a large bear. Shen has already sent a letter to Xu, the acting director of the zoo, saying that the large bear donated by Ueno Imperial Zoo will be transported to Shanghai by Director Shen when he returns to China. As for the origin of the bear, it is said to be from Northern Europe or Asia, larger than a bear, with yellow and white fur, a long neck, and short legs, and able to stand upright.

Thanks for the Peacock

At the same time, Shen enclosed his opinion in the letter, proposing to return a male fish-scaled peacock raised in the zoo to Ueno Imperial Zoo. Xu, the acting director, submitted a request to the Municipal Education Bureau, which has also approved it. The approval document stated that it was proposed to return a fish-scaled peacock to Ueno Zoo in Japan, requesting approval. The request has been approved. This is the order.

Zhuang Zhen Asks for Severe Punishment of Negligent Western Detective for Being Beaten and Humiliated After Reporting a Theft to the Police 137

Letters Sent to the Taxpayers Association and Ningbo Native Association Yesterday

Zhuang Zhen, the owner of Zhuang Mingji Electrical Company on Xiamen Road in this city, wrote to the Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Concession and the Ningbo Shanghai Native Association yesterday, saying: Greetings. The member has been running Zhuang Mingji Electrical Company at No. 116 Xiamen Road. On the evening of the 7th of this month, when checking the inventory in the store, it was suddenly found that four motors had been stolen, worth 300 yuan. After inquiring in various ways the next day, there was no trace. On the evening of the 8th, the member personally reported the discovery of the theft and requested investigation at the Laozha Police Station. Unexpectedly, a certain Western detective at the police station believed that the member was making a false report and refused to accept it. After the taxpayer member repeatedly stated the true situation, the two detectives showed an impatient expression, became annoyed, beat the member, and pushed him out the door. The member was innocently insulted and felt unwilling. Now the theft has been investigated by the member himself. It was done by a shop assistant named Wang. The original thief was arrested from the police station again on the 10th. This shows that the theft was a fact. The Western detective did not ask the reason and refused to investigate the theft of merchants and residents in his jurisdiction. He also beat and insulted the reporter for no reason. With such behavior, what is the use of taxpayers in the concession? The member's personal insult is a small matter, but it is a major matter related to the interests of the city's citizens. Therefore, a special letter is written, earnestly requesting your association to uphold justice and quickly forward it to the Public Works Department to investigate the negligent detectives and impose severe punishment to protect human rights and warn against illegality. Sincerely, I am extremely urgent. This is addressed to the Taxpayers Association of the Concession and the Ningbo Shanghai Native Association.

Long-Distance Cyclist Shi Wanli Arrives in Shanghai 138

Staying for Two Weeks, Going to Beijing Along the Shanghai-Nanjing Road, and Then Returning to Ping Along the Tianjin-Pukou Road Via Anhui and Shandong

Shi Wanli, a national long-distance cyclist, set out from Ping on June 6, 1934, passing through Henan, Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, Guangdong, and Guangxi, and then turning back to Guangdong, passing through Fujian and reaching Hangzhou, Zhejiang. He then traveled north along the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road and arrived in Shanghai yesterday (11th), traveling more than 20,000 miles in more than 20 months. He endured extreme hardships of wind, frost, rain, and snow along the way. Whenever he arrived in a place, he visited local schools and factories, and paid visits to local party and government authorities. Therefore, he obtained a wealth of materials and photos, and was deeply admired and assisted by authorities and celebrities everywhere, and was given certificates to introduce himself. After arriving in Shanghai, Shi plans to visit various factories, schools, and other institutions in the city, staying for about two weeks, and then starting again along the Shanghai-Nanjing Road to Beijing, crossing the river along the Tianjin-Pukou Road via Anhui and Shandong to return to Ping, completing all his work, and organizing the gains of this trip into a special book for the people of the country to consult.

Thief Falls to Death 139

Loose Wooden Window Unable to Bear Weight; Climber Met Gruesome End After Theft

At 5:30 AM yesterday, a thief, identified as Mr. Jia, attempted a burglary at the Tianxiangzhai Cake and Pastry Noodle Shop, located at No. 422 Avenue Edward VII. He climbed from the Yuqing Lane behind the shop into a third-floor guest room and stole a set of short coat and trousers and a bag of flour. The thief carried the stolen goods to the back window of the third floor, climbed out of the window, and grabbed hold of an iron bar, intending to climb down and escape. Unexpectedly, the wooden frame and cement encasing the iron bar on the window, having been weakened by age, could not bear the weight. The iron bar detached from the frame, and Jia fell from the height into the Yuqing Lane below. The back of Jia's head shattered upon impact, his brain matter splattered, and both of his thighs were broken. He was a bloody mess and died instantly upon hitting the ground. At that time, Lu Aquan and Dai Bingyi, employees of Tianxiangzhai, were already up and picking vegetables behind the shop. They suddenly heard a loud noise outside the back door. They opened the door to investigate and discovered that the third floor had been burgled and that the thief had fallen to his death. They immediately reported the incident to the street patrol, who reported it to the French Municipal Police Station. Detectives were dispatched to investigate, and the body was transported to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home for an autopsy. At 10 AM, they reported to Qiao Wanxuan, Chief Prosecutor of the Second Special District Court, who, accompanied by a forensic doctor and clerk, arrived at the funeral home at noon. The autopsy confirmed that the deceased was an unnamed male and that his death was due to injuries sustained from the fall. The case was officially registered. The patrol detective reported the details of the case and questioned Lu and Dai, the two witnesses, about their discovery. The official ordered the body to be handed over to the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home for photographs and burial.

Old Man Commits Suicide by Smoking Opium 140

Argument with Daughter-in-Law Leads to Tragedy

Zhou Aqi, a resident of the Yang Family Residence on the south bank of Yuncaobang in Wusong, was over seventy years old and had a longstanding opium smoking habit. He used to run a "Swallow's Nest" (opium den) in Songjiang for a living. After the January 28th Incident, due to his advanced age, he returned to his home in the Yang Family Residence and depended on his son, Xiao Fu, and grandson, Heshang, for support. The day before yesterday (the 10th), when Aqi got up in the morning, he had no hot water to wash his face, so he went to the kitchen to light a fire to boil water for washing and making tea. However, his daughter-in-law, Yang (i.e., Xiao Fu's wife), saw this and scolded the old man for wasting firewood. When the old man tried to argue, Yang, known for her unruly temper, started a quarrel. The old man, feeling angry and despondent, decided to end his life. In the afternoon, he swallowed raw opium. Later, he started moaning from the effects of the poison. His son and grandson discovered what had happened and tried to save him, but it was too late. He died around 7 PM. Yesterday, his son purchased a coffin and clothing for the funeral. Neighbors lamented that such an old man would take his own life over such a trivial matter.

Guang Shengli Leather Factory Fraudulent Liquidation Judgment 141

Deng Zhongze Sentenced to One Year Imprisonment

The Guang Shengli Leather Factory, located at No. 368 Tiantong Road, declared liquidation in June of the 21st year of the Republic (1932) due to the impact of the January 28th Shanghai Incident. Deng Zhongze, a Guangdong native, was appointed as the liquidator. The factory's creditors, Hong Kong Guangdong and local, amounted to over 600,000 yuan. The lawyers were Wang Siji and the accountants were Song Zhenchu. However, by December 31st of last year, Deng had inflated expenses, misappropriated funds, instructed Song to forge accounting records, and destroyed old ledgers. The case was exposed when shareholder He Jinlin reported it to the Hongkou Police Station. Deng was arrested and handed over to the First Special District Court on a 10,000 yuan bail. Later, it was discovered that he had embezzled over 20,000 yuan, and an additional bail of 10,000 yuan was required. Deng could not provide bail and was detained by the police. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao Shuangfeng presided over the continuation of the trial in the Third Criminal Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Municipal Council, stated that it had been verified that the defendant's liquidation office at No. 10 Daqing Lane, Nanjing Road, had inflated expenses for several years and had made false transfers through Mei Ya Company and Guang Shengfu and had also embezzled interest from deposits at the China Trust Company, totaling 21,547.71 yuan. He filed a public prosecution based on Article 336, Paragraph 1 and Article 210 of the Criminal Code (embezzlement and forgery of documents) and requested a severe punishment according to the law. The plaintiff also hired a lawyer to file a supplementary civil lawsuit, demanding the return of over 30,000 yuan in total. Judge Xiao questioned Deng thoroughly and sentenced him to one year imprisonment and a fine of 1,000 yuan. The supplementary civil lawsuit was transferred to the Civil Court of this court for trial. During the appeal period, the bail was reduced by 5,000 yuan.

Private Sale of Heroin, Rickshaw Driver Sentenced 142

Li Kuiyuan and Wang Yongqing Each Imprisoned for Six Years

Li Kuiyuan, from Qingjiang, residing at No. 9 Wu Family Lane in the French Concession, worked as a rickshaw driver. Wang Yongqing, Li's landlord, gave Li a bag of heroin and asked him to sell it. Li placed it in his rickshaw and was apprehended by detectives from the Zhabei Police Station. Wang was subsequently arrested. They were handed over to the First Special District Court for interrogation and the case was closed. Yesterday morning was scheduled for sentencing, but because further investigation was deemed necessary, the closing arguments were revoked. After the police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, presented the details of the investigation, Judge Qian Hongye interrogated Li Kuiyuan's maid, Qiaoyun, and the two defendants. After the police lawyer and the defendants' lawyers presented their arguments, Judge Qian announced the verdict: Li Kuiyuan and Wang Yongqing were each sentenced to six years of imprisonment and four years of deprivation of civil rights. The bag of heroin was confiscated.

Overview of the Shanghai Tung Oil Industry 144

— Chief Editor of China WeChat

(Thirteen in a Series of Overviews of Shanghai Industry and Commerce)

Our country's tung oil has always been centered in Hankou as a distribution market, with Shanghai being only secondary. Historically, the source of goods and the rise and fall of prices have depended on Hankou. Tung oil exports began in the second year of Guangxu in the late Qing Dynasty, but Shanghai only had Western companies trading for about ten years. After the European War, domestic sales of tung oil gradually declined, while exports increased year by year, placing it in an important position in international trade. In terms of the number of exports over the years, the peak was 754,081 quintals in 1933. In terms of value, the peak was 45,820,308 yuan in 1930. However, the actual trading volume of tung oil in Shanghai is only 60,000 to 70,000 dans per year, accounting for 6% of the total exports, so its position is not very important. But since the vigorous cultivation of Zhejiang tung and the large-scale sales in Shanghai, the situation has changed slightly, and Shanghai has gradually moved away from Hankou and become more independent. Now, I will first introduce the types and sources of tung oil:

Types and Sources of Tung Oil

Tung oil is extracted from tung seeds, which are produced by tung trees. This tung tree is called the oil tung, also known as the tung tree, and is a deciduous tree. Tung trees are divided into thousand-year tung and three-year tung. The former has an extremely long fruiting period and bears very few fruits, with harvests lasting for decades. The latter is the opposite, with the most abundant fruiting between the fourth, fifth, and sixth years, and gradually declining after the seventh year. Tung seeds are the kernels of the fruits of the tung tree. Approximately 40 to 50 catties of tung oil can be extracted from every 100 catties, called white tung oil. Most of China still uses traditional methods of oil extraction, which not only makes the oil quality easy to become turbid, but also causes a very heavy loss of oil volume. Tung oil can be divided into Sichuan tung, Southern tung, Xianggu tung, Bianjiang tung, Jingsha tung, Huizhou tung, and Zhejiang tung, according to the producing area. White tung oil is cooked in a pot and refined into a dark color, which is called Hong tung oil. If other oils are added, the quality becomes sticky and tenacious, which is called Xiu oil. Therefore, tung oil has three types of distinctions in terms of its nature: white, Hong, and Xiu, which is actually only the difference between raw and cooked. However, the packaging of tung oil varies, some are in barrels, and some are in baskets. At the same time, the quality of each type of tung oil also varies, so white oil is divided into Jingfang, barrel white, Zhichou, foot-degree oil, and basket-degree, and Hong oil is divided into regular and sub-brands, and Xiu oil is divided into sharp, medium, and tail. In addition, white, Hong, and Xiu are divided into the following brands:

1. White Oil – Chunyuan, Yichang, Hengchang, Dechang, Dechang, Maochang, Qichang, Yuchang, Yuchang.

2. Hong Oil – Xu Rongchang, Qing Yuanfeng, Yang Hengyuan, Ji Yingfeng, Ji Changhe, Heng Changyong, Xiang Taifeng, Ji Fengying, Xiao Hengqing, Yang Hengchang, Da Changfeng.

3. Xiu Oil – Wan Xingyu, Da Youheng, Ji Fengheng, Ji Taiheng, Da Youfeng.

Engaging in the tung oil business requires a thorough understanding of these complex distinctions. The source of tung oil is in the provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Sichuan, Shaanxi, Guangdong, Guangxi, Zhejiang, and Anhui, with an annual output of no less than 1.5 million dans. The transportation and sales of tung oil from each province is generally concentrated in Wanxian and Chongqing, and exported through Hankou. Guangdong and Guangxi are centered on Hong Kong, and Anhui and Zhejiang are centered on Shanghai. In the past, the source of tung oil in Shanghai, in addition to Hong and Xiu oils from the production area via Hankou, white oil also relied on Hankou. In 1923, Mr. Lu founded the Dongfang Oil Company, which operated in the Western trading style and began purchasing Zhejiang oil. Due to convenient transportation and high profits, other companies followed suit. As a result, the sales of Hankou tung oil in Shanghai were taken over by Zhejiang tung, and even the Hankou white oil sold in Shanghai is mostly adulterated with Zhejiang oil. Therefore, the Shanghai tung oil industry is gradually able to become independent from Hankou.

Sales and Transportation of Tung Oil

Before 1921, the sales volume of tung oil at home and abroad was equal, but after that they went in opposite directions. The foreign uses of tung oil are becoming more widespread, and in addition to general industrial uses, it also occupies an important position in military products, such as the outer layers of aircraft and submarines, which need tung oil for protection. On the other hand, domestic uses are limited to lubricating houses and appliances, and there is no development, so today, domestic sales are only about 16% of the total production, and 19 of the goods sold are substandard tung oil that is not suitable for export. The sales channels at home and abroad are described below:

1. Foreign Sales - China's tung oil is mostly exported to the United States, accounting for 70% of the total exports. The rest is sold to Britain, the Netherlands, Denmark, Germany, France, Belgium, Italy and other countries. In recent years, the United States has been cultivating tung trees itself in an attempt to resist Chinese oil, but the results are still few. Therefore, today China's tung oil exports can still maintain a monopoly position in the world market, which is even more evident in the table below:

China's Tung Oil Export Statistics Over the Years

Most of the foreign firms that purchase tung oil in China have offices in Hankou, Wanxian, Yuezhou, Changde and other places. The local firms are Hays, Heeyi, Anli, Jiali, Lihe, Shaohe, Jiacheng, Kobayashi, Sanyi and other foreign firms, but they are of a concurrent nature. (To be continued)

National Academy of Arts Traveling Troupe Arrives in Singapore: Overseas Chinese and Various Circles Hold Grand Welcome; Chinese Schools Jointly Hold Tea Party with Over Three Thousand Attendees; National Martial Arts and Basketball Performances to Be Held in Singapore for One Week 157

(Singapore Special Dispatch) The Nanyang Traveling Troupe, consisting of seventeen members from the Central National Martial Arts Academy and the National Physical Education Basketball Team, led by Chief Leader Pang Yusen, departed from Shanghai southward on the twelfth of last month and has already arrived in Singapore recently. Director Zhang Zhijiang of the Academy has also rushed from Europe to join the troupe. First, the Singapore Yiru Xuan Club held a welcome banquet. Subsequently, on the 30th of last month, the local Chinese schools jointly held a grand welcome meeting at the Great World Stadium, and it was decided that national martial arts and basketball performances would be held there the following day. Details of each event are recorded below:

Tea Party Welcome Circumstances. After the Nanyang Traveling Troupe arrived in Singapore, yesterday (the 30th), local Chinese schools jointly held a grand welcome meeting at the Great World Stadium. Representatives and students from twenty-six schools, including Overseas Chinese High School, Nanhua Girls' School, Guangyang School, Daonan School, Guangyu School, Zhendong School, and Lingnan Branch School, as well as over three thousand prominent figures from the community, attended. On that day, a tea party was held in the dance hall of the Great World, and a welcome meeting was held at the stadium, both presided over by Lin Yaoxiang, the principal of Overseas Chinese High School. During the tea party, Mr. Zhang Mingci from the Sanjiao Pu Mandarin Night School stood up and expressed his admiration. After the tea party, the director of the National Martial Arts Academy and members of the National Martial Arts Traveling Troupe took a group photo with the representatives of various welcoming parties as a souvenir. After the photo, the grand welcome meeting officially opened, with Zheng Zhaowu serving as the master of ceremonies. After the formalities, Principal Lin Yaoxiang of Overseas Chinese High School, on behalf of the schools, delivered a speech to Director Zhang and the National Martial Arts Nanyang Tour, expressing his admiration.

Zhang Zhijiang's Speech. After the speech, Director Zhang Zhijiang was invited to give instructions. Mr. Zhang's speech mainly stated that: National martial arts and the Chinese nation have equal significance. Only with the Chinese nation can there be national martial arts, and at the same time, only with national martial arts can there be the Chinese nation. National martial arts and the founding of the Chinese nation have a certain connection. We established our country in Asia. There are two elements to establishing a country. The first element is literature, and the second element is martial arts. Without literature, the country cannot exist, as everyone knows. Without martial arts, "without fists and courage, it is the root of disaster," and naturally it is not possible. Our Chinese history spans five thousand years, with a population of four hundred million and such a vast territory. The reason why we can pass it on from generation to generation and continue to exist is because we have literature and martial arts. Therefore, literature cannot be abandoned, and martial arts must be preserved without reservation. National martial arts is a kind of sport. This sport combines physical and practical use, strengthens the body and the race, and defends oneself and the country. However, it is unique to China. Foreign countries do not have it. Even the countries with the most developed sports in Europe and America do not have such sports.

National Martial Arts and Basketball Performances. After Mr. Zhang's instructions, members of the national martial arts troupe performed several sections of national martial arts, including fencing, broadsword versus spear, single saber versus spear, Taijiquan, and Bajiquan. The flashes of swords and the imposing atmosphere were breathtaking. The troupe also scheduled national martial arts and basketball performances at the Great World Stadium every night at 8:00 PM starting from the 31st. In basketball, the National Physical Education Basketball Team will compete against various teams that are pre-arranged by the Singapore Basketball and Volleyball Association on a daily basis, and the performances will continue for one week. Tickets are being sold for three yuan, two yuan, one yuan, and fifty cents, four types.

Municipal Literacy Education Committee Improves Inspection Methods for Literacy Schools; Offices in Each District Must Conduct Full-Day Inspections 167

The Municipal Literacy Education Committee has noted that most literacy schools enroll students in four or five classes, with different numbers of students and schedules in each class. As a result, the situation in each class varies greatly, and inspecting one or two classes cannot represent the entire school. Therefore, the committee has specifically ordered the offices in each district to conduct at least one full-day inspection of each literacy school per term, in addition to regular inspections, in order to thoroughly understand all aspects of the school's situation.

Franco-Chinese Friendship Association to Hold French Literature Award; Registration for This Year's Competition Begins Today 171

Since its establishment three years ago, the Franco-Chinese Friendship Association has spared no effort in carrying out its affairs. The association's previous holding of a literature award has already been reported in this newspaper. In order to encourage and promote Chinese culture, the association is now holding a French Literature Award with a prize of 500 yuan in national currency to be awarded to French works that study ancient or modern Chinese issues. The award regulations are recorded below: In order to promote Franco-Chinese cultural exchange, the association will award 500 yuan in national currency annually for French works. All French works that study ancient or modern Chinese issues may participate. Works participating in this award should be typed manuscripts or those published in the current year. The association's board of directors will appoint 10 to 15 members to form a judging committee to determine the award recipient. Judging committee members are not limited to members of the association and will not participate in the competition. The judging committee will use a secret ballot at the end of the meeting to decide the winner, in order to show solemnity. The judging committee has independent decision-making power regarding the award of the prize and may award the prize to one winning work or distribute it among several works. Any remaining prize money will be added to the prize money for the following year. Participants in this award are not limited by nationality or gender and should submit their works to the association's secretariat before December 1st each year. The award ceremony will be held publicly on May 30th. The association will make efforts to publish the winning work within its capabilities, with the copyright remaining with the author. Works participating in the competition will not be returned regardless of whether they win. Supplementary provisions: The registration period for the 26th year award competition is from today until December 1st of this year.

Children's Educational Novel Little Men (1)(7)(4) 176

— Original work by Louisa，Alcott, translated by Xiaocang

Mr. Bhaer laid down Rob, then rose and put his arm around the shoulders of his tall nephew, with a look of genuine pleasure on his face, and said:

"This thing can help me get through this suffering, and make me have a kind of trust in all of you. The town still needs me to take care of it, so I have to leave you for a few hours. I originally wanted to give you a day off, or send some of you home, but if you like to stay and continue as you were just now, then I think of my children, I will be very happy and proud."

"We would rather do it this way," "We want to stay," "Frank will take care of us"; several people shouted, and they were very happy to see that they had already gained Mr. Bhaer's trust.

"Isn't Mother March coming back"? Rob asked, showing a longing look; because without "Mother March" at home, as far as he was concerned, it was a world without sunshine.

"We two will come back tonight; but right now, good Aunt Meg needs her more desperately than you do, and I know you would be willing to lend her out for a while."

"Um, I'm willing; but Teddy has been crying for her all the time, he even hit Nansui, very badly and loudly," Rob replied, as if the news could urge his mother to return home.

Mr. Bhaer asked, "Where is my little man"?

"Don has taken him out to keep him quiet. He is nothing now," said Frank, pointing to the window with one hand, from which they could see Don dragging the little baby in his little car, with several dogs playing and jumping around him.

Overseas Cotton Prices Rise Simultaneously 183

Yesterday, American cotton opened higher, with all months rising by one to two points, with few transactions. There was demand for the March term from the same industry. Special Article

The Responsibilities of the Financial Sector in the Midst of Economic Panic 195

— Zhao Dihua

Since the European War, the economies of all countries have suffered significant losses. In order to restore pre-war prosperity and alleviate large-scale unemployment, they had to strive to open up foreign markets economically to increase international trade, in addition to political and diplomatic hostile camps. At the same time, in order to resist the dumping of products from other countries and protect their own industries, they also built high tariff barriers. This kind of economic warfare, in which each other reciprocated, became more and more serious over time, and economic panic swept the globe. Our country is no exception in the world trend. It is externally subjected to the pressure of changing currency policies and dumping markets in various countries, and internally affected by natural disasters, wars, and declining production. As a result, industry and commerce are exhausted, all industries are declining, and trade deficits are increasing year by year, forming a precarious situation.

Under the extreme decline of industry and commerce, the financial industry has made considerable progress. From 1931 to 1934, during these four years, the addition of banks was like bamboo shoots after a rain, constantly emerging. The annual increase in deposits and issuance, as well as the gradual increase in inventory surplus and other items, all indicate the forward march of China's banking industry. However, if we analyze the financial industry in more detail, we feel that the so-called prosperous situation is abnormal and contradictory. A country's funds are like blood vessels, and they must be connected to each other in order to fulfill their function. However, because the domestic area has lost its balance of payments under the dumping of imported products, and landlords and wealthy people have used cities as hidden pools, domestic funds have been concentrated in cities in recent years. As a result of the concentration, stagnation and accumulation of funds, the phenomenon of financial capital expansion and industrial capital depletion has also formed contradictory. Since the financial industry feels the accumulation of funds and their death in warehouses, it is difficult to recover industrial and commercial loans due to the decline of all industries. Therefore, operating highly profitable speculative businesses one day, financial stress will immediately see panic, and the rush of withdrawals will rise and fall one after another. The original funds of general banks with weak financial resources and unstable investments have been frozen, and they are increasingly unable to cope due to empty reserves. In the end, they have to close down and declare liquidation, which has formed the financial panic in recent years.

Under the current situation, industry and commerce should strive to strengthen the soundness of their own organizations and lay a foundation for a century with a long-term vision, and the financial industry should also seek further progress to assist in the improvement of the production industry in order to promote the development of the national economy. I will briefly describe what I have seen.

(1) Assist in Increasing Production and Reducing Imports

Many commentators believe that our country's trade deficit is a symbol of the decline of the national economy, which can fully demonstrate the backwardness of our country's industry and commerce over the years, and that if our country wants to save the economic panic, it must adjust the trade deficit. Our country is indeed the most important country with a trade deficit in the world, and the trade deficit is purely reverse, unlike countries such as the United Kingdom and Japan, which have large invisible incomes to compensate for the trade deficit. Since 1864, in 70 years, except for six years when there was a trade surplus, the rest were all trade deficits, and the numbers of the trade deficits increased with the year. The most was in 1932, reaching 556.06 million customs taels. In 1933 and 1934, although it was slightly reduced, it was also between 400 and 500 million yuan. The reduction in the deficit receipts in these two years was due to the failure to include the trade receipts of the Northeast Customs. The numbers of trade itself were low. One was due to the depletion of the domestic economy and weak purchasing power, and foreign goods failed to sell well, forming a phenomenon in which import trade receipts were lower than exports. It is not due to the development of export trade, or the progress of domestic industrial production, which is enough to replace the sales of foreign goods, so there is nothing to say that is satisfactory. The ratio of the trade deficit is equal to more than 50% of the total imports, and the severity of the situation can be imagined. The huge number of long-term trade deficits and total trade deficits over decades is unprecedented in various countries. Therefore, the trade deficit problem is a major difficulty in our country's current economy, and it is undeniable. (To be continued)
