Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 196

— (Yu Youqing)

Everything in the world is false, so the Buddhist scriptures say: "Form is emptiness, and emptiness is form." How insightful these two sentences are!

Originally, in this world, we come and go, which one is not false? Running to the doors of the powerful, vying for fame and fortune, which one is not false? When the king wants your life, you are still empty-handed. Isn't this the result of decades of busy work, still empty, still false?

Putting on a mask, no one can see whether you are Yao and Shun or a robber Zhi. Once it is exposed, you will know that you are completely false. This is the result of the last step of being a person.

The tone of a gambler, you "fake it," or say "don't fake it with me," seems to be a harsh warning, making the listener somewhat horrified. Because his own weakness seems to have been seen by others, he can no longer say false words, do false things, and put on false airs in front of others.

Many people often shout there: the sea of love is a sea of suffering, the field of love is a battlefield, and the gate of love is a difficult gate. We must not be overthrown by love or sacrificed for love. We must break everything and not enter the vortex to be a good man. But, but, although he said so, he has already been a prisoner in the field of love. Isn't this seeing through but not jumping over? As a result, words and deeds do not match, and it falls into the false way again.

Writing After Eating 197

— Wei Jing

What should one do after eating every day? This is a very worthy topic of study.

Dr. Hamilton, a medical doctor in California, USA, says that the best way to relax after a meal is to take a walk, play golf, or practice oriental boxing. (Note: This refers to our national martial art.) In short, one must exercise after a meal, but not engage in strenuous exercise, because lack of exercise after a meal easily leads to indigestion, while strenuous exercise after a meal can cause blood vessels to burst due to the already accelerated blood flow. This theory naturally represents a general view and is what we are most familiar with.

However, Dr. Goffman, a medical doctor from Germany, has a different opinion. He is strongly advocating for a half-hour nap after meals. He says that after eating, as blood circulation accelerates, the brain nerves often show signs of fatigue. At this time, even if any slight exercise can reduce fatigue to some extent, the brain nerves cannot help but increase fatigue because they have not completely calmed down all thoughts. Therefore, even after a considerable amount of recreation after a meal, one cannot work in the afternoon with the same energy as in the morning, which is clear evidence. To solve this problem, one should take a half-hour nap fifteen minutes after the meal to allow the whole body to rest completely. In that case, both body and mind will benefit, and one will be refreshed for work in the afternoon.

These two major schools of thought are in opposition. As for which we should follow, it is naturally impossible to say for now, because according to my observations in the office, some people stretch their legs on the desk and take a nap after a meal, while others go out for a walk in groups, but both sides are equally healthy. Some people neither take a nap nor take a walk, but simply gather together to tell jokes and talk about women, which is also very good. As for the ladies, it doesn't matter if they play eight rounds of mahjong after dinner every day. I wonder what foreign medical doctors would think of this?

Genuine Goods at Fair Prices 198

— Xu Haowu

The wind is rustling, the rain is bleak. As I was turning from the dark end of Xizang Road into Xinjiang Road, a "radiant" shop suddenly shone before my eyes.

Colorful electric lights tightly surrounded the perimeter of the horizontal signboard; beneath the signboard, a radio broadcasting vulgar tunes and local accents played incessantly, "Chinese learning for the fundamental principles, Western learning for practical application."

The spacious shop, except for a section enclosed by the counter to form a cold and quiet office area, was mostly occupied by goods displayed on the spot. In the center of the goods, under the intense light, leaned a wooden sign covered with a pasted-on red paper. Sparse words first stated that the shop had been established for many years and had a good reputation...finally: "If you can crack the following secret, you will know that our words are true:

"Seven people, eight eyes,

"Ten people, eight eyes,

"Outsiders, eight eyes,

"A Bao's mother also has eight eyes."

To prove that the riddle was not made up, countless narrow red strips of paper meticulously listed the types and prices of goods, making introductions and encouraging people to visit and compare as much as possible.

People occasionally paused, listened to the radio, and scratched their heads: "Price reductions without price reductions: price reductions without value, not more novel, but more palatable?"

Little Western Paradise 199

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 23: Eloquent Discussions Around the Room Lead to Litigation; Supplication for Reconciliation Leads to Old Friends Forgetting Past Grievances for Profit.

Bei Hai was originally unwilling to accept his hospitality, but seeing that he was being so particularly polite, he couldn't bear to offend him any further, so he laughed and said, "I really can't drink much alcohol. Three cups are out of the question. I'll just have one." Jia Duocai smiled and said, "Mr. Wang is a follower of the New Life Movement, no drinking, no smoking, which is very good. Everyone is happy today, and we must drink a little to express the joy in our hearts. Now, please have a cup, and I will drink three to accompany you." After giving this instruction, he held the kettle in his right hand and the wine glass in his left, pouring three cups in a row, all of which he drank in one gulp. Then, he picked up the empty cup and raised it, shining it at Bei Hai. Bei Hai smiled and watched as he held up the empty cup, keeping it raised as a reference, refusing to put it down. Bei Hai hesitated for a moment, then had no choice but to pick up his cup and drink it dry. Jia Duocai nodded repeatedly, saying, "Thank you." Afterwards, he clasped his fist at Bei Hai, saying, "Mr. Wang is too kind. To put it bluntly, we have already met before and can be considered old friends. If not for the relationship of old friends, you would not have been so generous. Come, come, let's fill Mr. Wang's cup again. As the saying goes, a thousand cups are too few when drinking with a friend." As he was saying this, he held the wine pot in his hand, wanting to pour wine for Bei Hai. Bei Hai was unwilling to acknowledge the words "old friend" in his heart, but he had already drunk the first cup of wine that had been poured for him. Could he really refuse the second cup that was being poured? So, he covered the wine glass with one hand and laughed, "I really can't drink anymore." Jia Duocai, holding the wine pot, still refused to take it back, laughing, "Pour it first, just to show the gesture. Surely, I can't force you to drink it, can I?" As he spoke, he shook the small copper wine pot in his hand. Bei Hai laughed, "Mr. Jia is truly skilled at persuading people to drink, making it impossible for me to refuse." So, he extended his wine glass to receive the cup of wine. Jia Duocai put down the wine pot, stood up, and bowed to Bei Hai from afar, laughing, "Mr. Wang's words truly make me undeserving. I won't force Mr. Wang to drink anymore in the future. Please, everyone, be at your leisure." Bei Hai laughed, "I will be at my leisure, and Mr. Jia need not be so polite." Jia Duocai gave a thumbs-up, saying, "Good! That's what friends are for." After finishing this sentence, he turned his head and saw that Wang Shicheng had been neglected on the side. He was holding his chopsticks, looking as if he wanted to pick them up but wasn't. He immediately realized that he hadn't even exchanged a few words with him, so he smiled and asked, "How is Mr. Wang's alcohol tolerance?" Shicheng laughed, "I don't drink." Jia Duocai gave another thumbs-up, saying, "I find Mr. Wang's words to be extremely straightforward. Based on this straightforwardness, I must invite you to drink two cups." (402)

Seen and Recorded 200

At the intersection of Avenue Road and Jiaozhou Road, that section of the road is probably going to be repaired, so the workmen from the Public Works Department painted red markings on the corner of the sidewalk and wrote the large characters "No Parking" at both ends of the right side of the road. In addition to Chinese, there was also a set of English words.

However, one day, I saw more than seven or eight cars parked in the restricted area. I really suspected that my eyes were deceiving me. I looked closely under the cars again, and indeed there were the four large characters "No Parking." It is common to see police officers urinating under the sign "No Urinating, Offenders Will Be Arrested." The situation here was similar. Next to the road was a Western restaurant opened by foreigners, and the people who came out of the cars were all foreign aristocratic women and distinguished gentlemen. Standing at the door were Western police officers, even sergeants, judging by their uniforms. But they were watching over the cars parked in the "No Parking" zone and the "gentlemen" who came out of them. Alas, the so-called law enforcers knowingly break the law. This is a common phenomenon throughout history and around the world.

A few years ago, I heard Mr. Wang Yunwu say: During American Prohibition, if a commoner secretly took a bottle of wine, he would be fined, but if gentlemen ostentatiously carried bottles of wine, the police would not dare to say a word. The world is generally like this!

Folklore>

Japanese Local Crafts 201

— Ji Yun

Our markets are filled with Japanese handicrafts. Apart from daily necessities, small crafts are the most common. These low-cost, high-profit items have greatly helped Japan's light industry develop and prosper. Every year, thousands of students from our country go to Japan to study and investigate, most of them to attend schools and conduct experiments. Very few go to factories and towns to study their small crafts. If someone could take the trouble to study them on the ground, they could greatly improve our small crafts when they return to the country. However, students studying in Japan spend a lot of money and always want to get a degree to get a promotion and make a fortune. Who would be willing to perform the farce of lifting a stone mortar?

Don't look down on local crafts as insignificant. You should know that local crafts are a local folk side business. If they can be improved and developed, they can stabilize the local economy. If the grass hats of Shandong, China, can be improved, they may be able to compete with those from Panama. If the Wuxi Afu dolls can change their style, they can compete with Japanese dolls. Moreover, our country has vast land and abundant resources. Almost anything can be used as raw material for handicrafts. Knowledgeable people look down on small crafts and are unwilling to study them. As a result, ignorant people stick to old methods, which will inevitably be eliminated. The old roosters and officials on the Jiangbei people's candy stands will probably remain the same after a hundred years.

(Explanation) It is said that at the beginning of spring at the hour of the dragon, the earth's energy shifts, and chicken eggs can stand upright on the ground. On the 5th of this month at three quarters past the hour of the dragon, it was exactly the beginning of spring. Mr. and Mrs. Zhang Zhengfan invited Man Yun, Xu Suling, Huang Jingzhai, Zhang Tianchou, Zhou Hanmei, and me, eight people in total, to conduct an experiment after breakfast. We took twelve chicken and duck eggs and went to the garden of the Tarashin Village to wait until three quarters past the hour of the dragon. Each of us tried with an egg, and it really worked. Mr. Zhang also took a photo, as shown in the picture on the right. At the time, it was considered a strange tale. Half an hour later, we tried again, but the eggs fell over immediately. This shows that the legend is not false. We specially record this in the hope that scientists will provide a scientific explanation and send it to this publication for further disclosure. (Ji Ping)

Everyone knows that Japanese industry is developed, but apart from large factories with large chimneys and large sites, most ordinary factories use small electric machines. They only have a dozen workers and less than ten rooms. Our factories look impressive, with a tiger head sign hanging outside that says "Factory Restricted Area, No Trespassers," but in reality, it's just a facade. The factory's assets have long been mortgaged. Building factories economically and installing more machines saves capital and labor costs, which is the basic principle of Japanese small industry. Regardless of the factory, they all hire knowledgeable specialists to design and create patterns. As a result, everyone is scheming and competing with each other with originality. Therefore, their products emerge endlessly and keep up with the times. On the one hand, when new products appear in Europe and the United States, they study and imitate them, and the results are often better and cheaper than those of Europe and the United States.

In coastal areas, shells are produced. Nearby families pick up beautiful shells and make them into toys. Two shells combined become the belly of a bird, and the head of a snail shell can be made into various different birds. Ornaments carved from clam shells are white and shiny, similar to our ivory carvings. Our family chemical company's clam honey utilizes nature in the same way. In Japan, storing food and toys in large clams is also the same. Clay figures are as modern as reality. The clay figures are dressed in beautiful silk clothes and have already become objects of appreciation for adults rather than just toys for children. They can imitate men and women of all countries, and actors and stars are their models. First, artists carve models based on photos, and then gradually reproduce them. Each person's clothes and posture are based on magazine photos. Therefore, they have a strong appeal when placed in the showcase. Anyone who walks past wants to stop and admire them. The highest prices reach over one hundred yuan.

There are countless kinds of celluloid toys and iron and wooden trains and cars. Recently, celluloid dolls have also been dressed in tulle clothes, which adds a lot of beauty. In addition, the bodies are equipped with clockwork, allowing them to walk and swim. These small crafts cannot be learned in school. You can only collect and buy them in various places to study and improve them. If our small factories want to compete with Japanese goods, they must first ask someone to collect them, and then imitate and improve them. This is twice the result with half the effort.

It can be said that there is no place in Japan without local products. This shows the development of local crafts. Hokkaido produces wood, so they use various tree barks and branches to make stationery, which is also simple and lovely. In some places, bears are produced, so the people carve bears out of wood and turn them into decorations. Other crafts such as bamboo work, lacquer work, and wheat straw work are all very interesting. Because the patterns and styles are constantly striving for novelty and beauty, they can attract customers. Suppose there is a cigarette case made of porcelain, tin, wood, bamboo, glass, pottery, shells, etc. In addition to glass and tin, the lampshades for electric lights come in several types, including silk, printed paper, celluloid, and bamboo frames. Their crafts are beautiful and harmonious in color and up-to-date in style. They are all modern utensils and will never stick to old methods. Recently, the Japanese have been paying close attention to the war between Italy and Abyssinia. They have taken advantage of this and have already manufactured many black soldiers for sale.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Medical Lecture

Various Treatments for Gonorrhea 202

— Dr. Feng Shanliang

The medicines and instruments for treating gonorrhea have become dazzling in modern times. However, analyzing the treatments, there are no more than four types. What are these four types? They are: (1) Oral medication. One should choose excellent preparations with strong penetrating power and anti-inflammatory and bactericidal properties. For example, "Metsalin," sold by the German-owned Meihe Trading Company, can be said to be flawless in these aspects. (2) Local therapy. Silver protein and other preparations are usually used to make local irrigation solutions. When using this type of therapy, if the duration of use and the concentration of the solution are not appropriate, it can be said to be ineffective. Since the invention of "Gonorrhea Soother" by the German Manerzhi Pharmaceutical Factory, many in the medical and pharmaceutical fields have switched to using it because it is a mixture of gonorrhea serum and Soother, which has the effect of immunizing and curing gonorrhea. (3) Injection therapy. Injections of pigments and mixed gonorrhea vaccines. Good preparations of pigments include Terupafflavin from Tiande Pharmaceutical Factory, and excellent mixed gonorrhea vaccines include "Manerzhi Turbid Mixture Vaccine" from the German-owned Gaofu Trading Company. These two use medicinal power to kill bacteria and automatic immunization, respectively. Using them alternately can be said to be appropriate. (4) Electrical therapy. Based on heat sterilization, the so-called diathermy sterilization, shortwave diathermy is the most valuable. The use of Furke's purple light electricity and long-wave diathermy is difficult to achieve satisfactory results, and may even prolong the recovery period, not to mention the drawbacks of burning the skin. In addition, for urethral gonorrhea, meaning that the symptoms are entirely in the urethra, irradiation with cold light from a mercury quartz lamp, the so-called photosterilization, also has considerable effect.

The Harmful Effects of Opium on the Human Body and Its Withdrawal Symptoms 203

— Physician She Lei

Anyone addicted to opium must consume a certain amount of opium every day, otherwise, withdrawal symptoms will appear immediately (commonly known as "detox"). I will briefly describe several types as follows: (1) Increased secretions. The secretions of the lacrimal glands, salivary glands, and mucous glands of the upper respiratory tract all increase sharply. The most obvious manifestation is tearing. (2) Gastrointestinal disorders, such as belching, vomiting, and diarrhea. (3) The reproductive organs also undergo significant changes, such as excessive menstruation in women and spermatorrhea and increased libido in men. (4) Insomnia. This type of insomnia cannot be effectively treated with hypnotics. (5) Changes in the circulatory system. The pulse becomes weak and rapid. In severe cases, it can lead to collapse or death from heart failure. (6) Others, such as yawning, sneezing, and aching limbs. The reason for these phenomena is the result of opium harming the human body. All chronic opium addicts have these phenomena. The harmful effects of opium can be divided into mental and physical aspects. The mental aspects are difficult to describe, so I will omit them. As for the physical aspects, those that can be demonstrated by objective observation include: (1) Lack of subcutaneous fat. The skin is loose and sagging. Nine out of ten smokers are thin all over. Those with severe addiction are even worse. (2) Secretions are all impaired. The secretions of the salivary glands and sebaceous glands are reduced. This can be inferred from dry skin. The secretions of the digestive glands are also impaired. This can be inferred from loss of appetite, indigestion, and irregular bowel movements. (3) Reproductive function is also weakened, such as impotence in men and amenorrhea in women. (4) Changes in the circulatory system are also significant. The pulse is slow and irregular. If the source of opium toxins can be reduced or eliminated, it will not be difficult to eliminate the above symptoms and restore the original healthy state.

Skin diseases are highly contagious. The most common are ringworm and scabies. Bathing together, anything that can directly contact the skin, even with slight carelessness, can be infected. Spermatorrhea and Premature Ejaculation 207

— Sun Zhiyao

Spermatorrhea and premature ejaculation are both symptoms of sexual neurasthenia. Most cases of this disease are caused by excessive sexual activity and masturbation. Human semen is most precious. Its source is the testicles, and it is used by the epididymis to transport it to the seminal vesicles. Part of it flows into the lymphatic vessels to the blood vessels and circulates in the blood as nutrition, and part of it returns to the testicles through the arteries to become semen again. Semen circulation, excessive spermatorrhea, and excessive masturbation and sexual activity can cause excessive consumption of semen. The new blood produced physiologically is insufficient to replenish it. As a result, premature ejaculation and spermatorrhea, even the nervous system, are affected, leading to neurasthenia. Not only that, but other diseases such as brain disease and heart disease will also follow. Therefore, spermatorrhea and premature ejaculation must never be ignored, as they can endanger life. The treatment for this disease can be said to emphasize both medication and mental health. Such as correct thinking, abstinence from desires, avoiding overwork, strict adherence to hygiene, and choosing nutritious foods. The use of drugs, such as organic phosphorus and endocrine, are considered reasonable. "Anershen," a mixed preparation of these, is highly recommended by the medical and pharmaceutical communities. Questions and Answers About Illnesses 208

— Editor

This column is dedicated to your inquiries. You are welcome to send us letters with any questions you have about illnesses. We will take responsibility for providing concrete answers. In your letters, please concisely explain your condition, treatment history, etc. Send to the editorial department at Shanghai Post Office Box 1668. If you do not want your questions to be published in the journal but require a written reply, please include postage of two cents for local replies or five cents for replies outside of Shanghai.

Solution Leakage

(Question from Mr. Xu Yingnan) I used to suffer from spermatorrhea, but I recovered a long time ago. Recently, I suddenly noticed a white, milky liquid leaking from my urethra, but it is very sparse and painless. I cannot identify the disease and would like to know what medicine to use to treat it.

Answer: This is a symptom of chronic gonorrhea. In addition to extreme self-care, you can use "Miesha Lin" internally and "Lindu Shule'er" externally for drug treatment, and you should be able to recover on your own.

Pregnancy or Illness

(Question from Mr. Lu Naikang) A relative of mine is 32 years old and had a difficult birth six years ago. According to the doctor at the time, her uterus had a problem. For several years since then, she has had no other problems except for slight discomfort during menstruation. Recently, her period has stopped for three months. I don't know if it is pregnancy or illness. Please advise.

Answer: Based solely on your letter, I cannot make a definitive judgment. Please consult a gynecologist or undergo a pregnancy test. Dr. Hayes, a German medical doctor specializing in gynecology, is on the second floor of Chunzai Hospital at 66 Ningbo Road in the French Concession of Shanghai. You can go there for a diagnosis.

Long Time Without Bathing

(Question from Mr. Ni Liuru) I previously suffered from a venereal disease and have not bathed for a long time. After the venereal disease healed, my skin developed severe itching. The itching is worse when I am in a warm bed at night. Looking at the itchy area, there are only small, goosebump-like particles. It seems like scabies but not scabies, like ringworm but not ringworm. I don't know what disease it is and what medicine I should use.

Answer: Try applying "Miejue Jun." This medicine is a sacred product among skin disease treatments. It is effective in treating all kinds of skin diseases.

Profuse Leukorrhea

(Question from Mr. Xu Fangren) Unfortunately, I contracted leukorrhea last summer and, due to an accident, did not receive thorough treatment, which affected my wife. Now she has profuse leukorrhea, even worse than before. Please recommend a good doctor and provide a treatment plan.

Answer: Dr. Liu Xuannv of Chunzai Hospital on Ningbo Road in the French Concession of Shanghai specializes in treating women's uterine diseases. You can go there for treatment. Also, treatment medications for this condition, such as internal use of "Miesha Lin," external use of "Lindu Shule'er," and injections of Mannal old spermatorrhea fluid seedlings, are all considered reasonable.

Frequent Abdominal Pain

(Question from Mr. Li Yujin) I have always had stomach problems, which often cause abdominal pain. I have seen doctors and taken medicine, but they are only temporarily effective, and the pain recurs. I don't know how to treat it or what medicine is best to permanently eliminate this problem. Please advise.

Answer: You can take "Wei Bao," a preparation from Yaljiali, for stomach pain. However, you still need to continue taking it for a while after recovery. You must also avoid certain foods, such as alcohol, vinegar, spicy foods, and all other irritants.

Talks

Committing Suicide out of Concern for the Country 209

— Tai

Committing suicide out of concern for the country is naturally something worth a passionate and tragic song. From the perspective of suicide itself, suicide is such a serious and sad thing. To willingly sacrifice oneself out of concern for the country is such a moving and admirable act. Such things seem worthy of worship and admiration. However, I say no, absolutely not.

Why? In China, many things have very pleasant names, but the reality is not so. Not only the suicide of Supervisor Du Yangzhi out of concern for the country, which is not worth mentioning, but even the sensational act of Xu Fanting cutting open his stomach to pay tribute to the mausoleum cannot be said to be the act of a hero. Because suicide is passive, it is boring. Even if one commits suicide, it cannot be said that the goal of concern for the country is fully achieved. It is truly a case of worrying for nothing and killing oneself for nothing.

If a person who commits suicide has such spirit and such courage, then there is much that can be done in the world. Since one is going to die anyway, one might as well do something sensational and die, which can benefit the country, leave a name for posterity, and stimulate the people's eyes and ears. How valuable is this? The ancients said, "Death can be heavier than Mount Tai or lighter than a feather," which is what is meant here.

People especially suffer from fear of death. If one is afraid of death, there is nothing that can be done. The heroes, brave men, famous generals, and outstanding figures in history, which of them did not get their titles from not being afraid of death? Therefore, not being afraid of death is originally the best thing, but there are reasons for not being afraid, and death has its price, so that one's death is not in vain.

Therefore, although I feel a kind of compassionate enthusiasm for the general public who commit suicide out of concern for the country, I absolutely cannot consider them to be ambitious and capable people.

Old Wandering Song 210

— Liang Qiyun

I worked at the Xinhua Fan-tan gambling den—its beautiful name is the Xinhua Club—for less than three months and it was over again. At first, I fully thought that from now on I could live a good life, but this beautiful, spring flower-like hope finally sank to the bottom of the sea without a sound, like throwing a stone into the vast ocean.

That night, there were a dozen of our buddies and forty or so gamblers in the detention center of the Fifth District Police Station. Everyone stared at each other blankly, you looking at me, I looking at you, it was really boring, and we couldn't even talk a little. Later, everyone leaned against each other and dozed off. We spent the night like this, and continued until the afternoon of the next day before we were released. The verdict was a large fine, which was paid by our boss.

I decided not to do this kind of thing again. I wasted a lot of days wandering around aimlessly. During those days, I joined their group—Blackie Chen, Tall Li, and Ah-Kei's organization—and partnered to peddle "Hundred Herbs Panacea Oil" on the streets.

Because I joined their group later, and the capital I paid was only three silver dollars. In fact, they were all Blackie Chen's ideas, and he only told me to take the flag with the words "Liu Bohui Hundred Herbs Panacea Oil" written in eight bowl-sized white characters, and carry the medicine box.

Every day, I wandered from the beginning of the street to the end, my feet were sore from running, my mouth was dry from shouting, and then I could eat those two bowls of plain rice. Although it was such an interesting business, haphazardly mixing several kinds of medicines together and saying that they were made from a hundred herbs, which could cure all kinds of diseases. The hundred kinds of herbs, even I couldn't figure out. —People sometimes need to deceive other people with fake things.

However, often in the quiet of the night, thinking of others and looking at myself, I would feel sad about an unfortunate thing that human power could not undo, looking at the vast sky with eyes that doubted everything in the world, cursing fate. The situation was just like a flock of crows returning to their nests, flying over the river and casting a dark and vast shadow, and my heart would become inexplicably dark.

Soon, my cousin found me a job as a gatekeeper in a middle school. Without hesitation, I left those three partners.

"Good fortune will not come to me."

I often thought like this when I was unhappy.

Really, in just five months, because I secretly took some students' money and let them go out to play, I was fired.

I was somewhat at a loss.

Nothing worked out, and the days passed one by one. What made me most anxious was the problem of eating. I couldn't not eat, and for this, I had done many dishonorable things. … Gradually, the days became a little hard to get through. At first, I struggled hard as if suffocating. One day after another passed, like a camel trudging through the gray journey in the desert, so hard that sometimes I couldn't even breathe. It was as if a rope was tied around my head, and when it loosened, I gasped painfully, and when it tightened, even…

(Life is a bad thing that respects the strong and bullies the weak!)

(Do you understand?)

Many relatives and friends, devout worshipers of life, would see you, this poor wretch, and secretly say in their hearts,

—Let's give him the cold shoulder, this kid doesn't bring anything good when he comes to the door.

Then, they would grumble and curse indirectly.

Even if my stomach was empty, it was difficult to freeload a meal. …

Because I was bored, I often went to the Pearl River to stroll around. Leaning on the railing, I could see the broad face of the Pearl River. The river water flowed as if it would never feel tired. When it was lively, it would sing softly little tunes that people didn't know; when it was silent, it would make people feel scared. It was like a sick old man, thinking that the message of death was coming soon.

Far away, the Haizhu Iron Bridge posed with the air of a noble and arrogant gentleman. Ships loaded with goods, people, shuttled back and forth. Some brought from the distant sky devils sucking the blood of this mysterious old country; others carried from old villages and towns batches of things that sold out the glory of their ancestors.

On the shore, high-rise buildings stood tall.

In the heart of the river, if one or two warships of unknown purpose stayed, there would be huge purple shadows, inverted in the water, and the shadows also liked to joke with the ripples on the water.

I loved to stare blankly at those things with my tired eyes. At the same time, I felt a shadow in my heart, gradually, gradually, expanding. I worried that this shadow would erode my fragile heart one day.

Such wandering was not entirely bad. Walking around the doorways of those cargo warehouses, I occasionally found a chance to be a temporary porter and earn enough to eat a meal.

However, day after day, wandering in the emotions of worry, resentment, emptiness, and depression, a person continued to live almost like a ghost.

—Tired, right?

If I could still feel happy, it would be when I had escaped it—this life guarded by the devil. Yes, no one cannot realize that every prisoner longs to escape from prison. …

This continued for another eight or nine months. —

Until later, when I received a letter from my uncle in the Yangloudong tea mountain, telling me to go to him immediately, I resolutely ended this "journey of life" and embarked on another new one.

Candy 211

— Hu Weixiong

Returning from a friend's house, I passed a newly opened candy store. The tender green paint, illuminated by the dozens of extremely bright electric lights in the store, looked very harmonious and beautiful… I take this road home every day, but I can't remember whether this storefront was closed before or was another shop. Because it was newly opened, the store was crowded with customers, surging in and out in a disorganized way. Walking on the street, I only saw the clerks' heads moving back and forth above the customers' heads. At this time, a pedestrian in front of me suddenly stopped in front of the store, so I also stopped, and naturally others stopped behind me. Speaking of which, I have disliked eating candy since I was a child. Now I have teeth that can crack walnuts in one bite, which my mother says is because I don't eat candy. Today, I went to my friend's house to discuss an event that has a great relationship with my future. The result was a failure, but on the way home, I never forgot about this matter. I thought that perhaps my words were not sincere enough, or that I should use a roundabout method to move my friend's heart and make him help me complete this matter. Thinking like this, I felt very regretful and sad. Although I was not sure whether I could succeed by doing so, it seemed as if this matter had not been completed. I almost wanted to go back to my friend's house. While wandering alone, trying to find a solution, I just stopped in front of the candy store, and watching the person in front of me step into the store, I also stepped into the crowd as if drawn by him. Didn't I say that I never liked eating candy? I don't understand what I came in here to do? In the center of the store, there was a very beautiful tower, built from many different styles of cookies, adorned with small five-colored electric lights, but so many people were calling out to the clerks for something, not paying attention to the tower of lights. I admired this work of art like a connoisseur. I don't know if I looked like a pickpocket at that time. A clerk with a stiff collar and half of his white shirt sleeves rolled up ran up to me and asked what I wanted to buy. At this time, I really had no reason to refuse him, because many customers were crowding around him, asking him to wrap up some candy names that I was not familiar with, so I replied that I wanted to buy something. He led me to another counter, pointing to various beautiful boxes and plates inside the glass cabinet. These were all foods that I had never paid attention to before. Now, under the clerk's courteous service, I haphazardly pointed to this and that, asking him to wrap up a little. But when I wanted to ask him the price, he grabbed a lot of samples from inside, some pine nut candies, some coconut candies, some small individual pieces, some square pieces. I was surprised that I had learned so much knowledge about candy today, and asked him to wrap up a little of each kind, totaling more than three dollars. Carrying such a large bundle of things, I could not walk, so I called a rickshaw to go home.

My wife was waiting for me at the door. I had just noticed that the street lights at the entrance of the lane were already on. Because there were too many electric lights on in the candy store, I forgot that I had spent a lot of time there. Seeing me carrying a large bundle of things home, my wife took it with one hand. When she clearly saw the four characters "Tianlu Zihao" on the sign paper, she smiled innocently and asked me what I was so happy about that I bought so many talented candies. She seemed to realize that the matter discussed with my friend had achieved unexpected success, and called the child's name and ran upstairs. I paid the rickshaw fare and slowly went upstairs, feeling as if I had a dream, but that large bundle of candy was clearly being unwrapped by the child, one bag after another. I asked myself in my heart why I bought so much candy?

Temptation - Radio Drama Script by Drama Actors (6) 212

— Scripted by Liu Yawei

Older Brother: These are probably refugees who escaped from the village ahead! Alas! Wives and children scattered! (Sound of wind and rain)

A-Qiao: Older brother, the house is about to collapse! (Sound of metal, sound of knocking on the door, asking who?)

Old Zhang: Older brother, older brother! Open the door quickly! (Door opens)

Little Lu: What's wrong?

Old Zhang: (Panting) Let's prepare quickly! The village ahead needs immediate support! The flood is so fierce, many people have died! The embankment cannot be strengthened. Originally, hundreds of strong men were blocking the breach, but now most of them have been swept away by the water!

(Distant sound of a gong ringing urgently) (Singing) Everyone sheds blood and sweat together, not afraid of aching muscles and bones to survive… (Faint singing) Hng yo!…

Older Brother: The sound of the gong in front of the Earth God Temple is ringing. Little Lu, Old Zhang, quickly pick up your hoes and go to assemble! A-Qiao, don't be sad, show some courage, take the two packages to Old Wang's place and wait for us. (Loudly) Open the door! (Wind and rain) Go, go! (Sound of people running around, sound of iron hoes and rakes) Go, go! (Everyone also shouts) Assemble at the Earth God Temple, we can't wait for anyone to help us now, we can only rely on ourselves to save our own lives! (Sound of the gong getting closer, sound of people, sound of iron rakes and hoes)

Old Wang: Brothers, come and assemble quickly, the flood in the village ahead is about to engulf our village, if we escape, we will starve to death, if we don't escape, everyone go forward and strengthen the embankment, at least we can block the breach, if we work together and try our best, our fields will definitely be saved, everyone get up, unite, and swear not to retreat! Save our survival, resist our bad luck! We still have to rely on ourselves!

(Everyone shouts in support) (Older brother leads the crowd in shouting):

(Sound of wind, rain, running, iron gong, shouting)

Unite! Everyone get up! Swear not to retreat! Save our survival! Resist our bad luck!

(Sound of many people, sound of water, sound of blocking the breach) The sound of living people being swept away by the water and shouting wildly! This place should be acted out realistically!

Opening Chapter "Dream of the Red Chamber" "Daiyu Mourns Autumn"

Wutong leaves fall, it's the beginning of autumn. Daiyu is, touched by the scenery, with a thousand feelings. I think, my delicate face is extremely thin. Listening to that, the autumn insects chirping in the crowd. Like autumn rain sprinkling over the world. Seeing that, the autumn dew is like a pearl, easily extinguished. Like a bubble in water. Thinking that life is like morning dew. Turns into emptiness like dusk smoke. I see things hurt my heart and ache. Can't help but, jade chopsticks shed tears. More than the spring cuckoo cries.

spirit, and is recognized as a rare and excellent set designer in the Chinese film industry. He has contributed significantly to the Chinese film industry in the past decade or so. Now, his long-held directorial aspirations have finally been realized, and "Incarnation Girl" is his first work.

Wu Cun Directs a Scene from "Spring Flower" 218

Information from the Chinese Film Gengsu Society 219

The Chinese Film Gengsu Society, after recently moving to its new address at Room 204, Taihe Building, Laohe Road, is actively expanding its activities. On the one hand, it is holding a general meeting of members to solicit opinions, and on the other hand, it is expanding its recruitment of male and female members. Anyone who loves film and drama can join, making it a venue for the public to study film.

The "Sightseeing Tour," "Book Department," "Chess Competition," "Army, Navy, and Air Force Chess Competition," "Film and Drama Discussion Group," and other activities that are being decided upon will all be established and implemented in the shortest possible time.

Chang Shaobai put a lot of thought and effort into the color scheme of the society's emblem before finally achieving a satisfactory design. The design is a complete blue map of China, with a bright red star marking Shanghai, indicating that the base is in Shanghai. A silver-white ray of light emanates from the star. It is said that these three beautiful colors of blue, white, and red have the same brilliance as the national flag, and also contain the meaning of "Chinese film advancing" and "great spirit."

Tian Chen, an artistic dramatist, has now been hired by Chang Shaobai to serve as a dance instructor. He is dedicated to the art of dance and is not only proficient in various ballroom dances but also excels in solo and tap dances on stage.

"Incarnation Girl" - A Treasure 220

— Yu Lin

Han Langen - this only outstanding comedian in the Chinese film industry, with an awkward face, the number one precious item, in Yihua Company's new sound film "Incarnation Girl" directed by Fang Peilin, plays Yuan Meiyun's cousin, that is, a foolish, clumsy, mischievous, and extremely greedy rich young man. In other words, he is the treasure in "Incarnation Girl." His humorous movements and expressions undoubtedly bring a more relaxed and lively atmosphere and mood to "Incarnation Girl."

Shen Bao Local Supplement Automobile Special Issue

The New 1936 Buick Automobile (Part 1) 222

— Dan

The new 1936 Buick automobile is exquisite. Everyone who has seen it and ridden in it praises it unanimously.

Originally, its fame was not accidental. Because of its new silent straight-eight cylinder overhead valve engine, plus the unique "Annorite" pistons, it has extraordinary functions. Its strong power and convenient driving are also obvious. Its contribution to economy can be quickly proven. Other features, such as the "toe-tap" vacuum braking system, the Fisher "Turret Top" steel body, the enlarged space and increased comfort, as well as the sophisticated machinery and the beautiful interior and exterior, are all extraordinarily obvious. The above characteristics are all closely related to the riding public. I will talk about its main points in the following article.

As the saying goes, seeing is believing. Readers, if you want to know the benefits of Buick cars, it is best to actually ride in a Buick and let Buick itself demonstrate it to you personally. But even now, though it is armchair strategy, one can roughly outline its major points.

First, let's take a look at the entire Buick car, which is divided into four groups and fourteen models, suitable for all places and all walks of life.

Ninetieth Series "Limited" Model This Buick car is large and low, and extremely spacious. The width exceeds the height. During manufacturing, all previous dimensions were abandoned, and a new path was taken, sparing no effort to make its style and splendor take the lead in the automotive world for one year.

Eightieth Series "Roadmaster" Model With a gorgeous appearance and superior horsepower, it can be called a double masterpiece. No matter when or where, it runs smoothly and comfortably, without any bumps or vibrations. Calling it "Roadmaster" is truly living up to its name.

Sixtieth Series "Century" Model This Buick car has higher horsepower and speed than usual. It can only be compared to a whirlwind. Countless people in society are eagerly awaiting the appearance of this car. Now, without paying a high price, they can get a car with unparalleled horsepower and speed, while its exquisite style, beautiful appearance, and excellent quality are not inferior. It can be said that their wish has come true.

Fortieth Series Special Many car passengers often dream of buying a Buick car, but due to price concerns, they have not been able to fulfill their wish. There are also many people who, once they bought a Buick car, have been struggling financially in recent years due to environmental factors, making it impossible for them to keep it. Now their dreams can come true, because the Special Buick is very low in price, so even those who are not very wealthy can afford it. Moreover, its quality is still exactly the same as the higher-priced cars. All the characteristics of Buick are fully possessed by the Special Buick, and these characteristics are not found in other cars in the world.

The above are the four groups of new Buick cars. The streamline of each car, from the new narrow radiator grille to the rear bumper, extends in an unbroken line. Its horsepower and speed are unprecedented. Parking such a car in front of the mansion is truly impressive.

Let's take a look at the car roof again, which is closely integrated with the body, like a seamless garment. This is the Fisher "Turret Top" style roof, made of seamless cold-drawn pure steel. Also, the chrome on the hood shines brightly, which is also a feature of Buick cars. Other features, such as chrome radiator trim, strong spoked wheels, wide foot pedals, and the trunk integrated with the body, are all special features. Everything in each car is pleasing to the eye and moving.

Inside the Buick car, the driving area is very spacious. The slanted seats are deeper and wider than before, and the headroom is extremely generous. Here, another change can be seen, that is, the brake lever has been moved from the usual place to under the partition, to the driver's left, which is the easiest place to reach. The space at the feet is therefore very generous.

The chrome instrument panel is also a lovely thing. The numbers on the speedometer and other gauges can be read at a glance, even when driving very fast. The instrument panel can also emit light directly or indirectly for night driving. A small red light on the partition lets you know whether the headlights are bright or dim. This convenience has also been long desired in the automotive world.

Before we talk about driving, let's take a look at the rear. The seats are wider, the headroom is higher, and the legroom is more generous. The rear seats are soft and comfortable, which is truly delightful. Its slope and shape have been carefully studied and are perfectly suited for rest. The cushions, lining, door handles, and other accessories are perfectly matched.

We have already looked at the interior, and now we are ready to drive. The engine is already running, but you can hardly hear its sound.

A Review of the US Trucking Industry Last Year 223

— Mo Ya

Truck transportation has its own unique advantages, which have long been well known to users. As a result, freight trucks in the United States are among the most advanced and developed of all modes of transportation in terms of production and use. A look back at the production of freight trucks in the United States last year—1935—will make this particularly clear.

At the end of 1935, US automobile factories manufactured no fewer than 725,000 freight trucks in total. This number is an increase of 21 percent compared to 1934. As a result, the production volume in 1935 was the most developed of all years except for 1929, and it was only slightly different from 1929. The production volume from January to August 1935 was 535,041 vehicles.

In addition to domestic use and domestic market needs, US freight trucks also occupy a very important position in other markets. The number of vehicles exported from the United States to Europe, the Far East, Africa, and other regions each year is also considerable. Exports of freight trucks in 1935 increased by 21 percent compared to 1934. It is estimated that no fewer than 193,000 freight trucks were exported in 1935, accounting for one-quarter of the total production volume.

Why is the freight truck industry so developed? There is also a very important reason for this. According to research by government agencies, the following advantages have been discovered: Economy. The price of cars and gasoline in the United States are not very high, and a single truck can carry a lot of cargo. As a result, using freight trucks is cheaper than using other modes of transportation. Fast service. This is something everyone can agree on. The loading and transportation of goods by truck is always faster than by other means. Convenient delivery. The advantage of trucks over trains is in the convenience of delivery. Because train stations are often far from the city, goods cannot be delivered immediately upon arrival at the station. The situation with freight trucks is different. They can deliver goods directly to the recipient's door. This is its characteristic. Although freight trucks account for only one-eighth of the total number of registered vehicles in the United States, they pay one-quarter of the special vehicle tax. This shows the development of freight trucks.

According to a survey by the American Automobile Manufacturers Association, there are 48,000 villages and towns in the United States that do not have railroad service. As a result, all transportation relies entirely on automobiles. The population of these villages and towns accounts for 7 percent of the national population. As a result, in the past 25 years, their ability to connect with major urban areas has been entirely dependent on the great contribution of automobiles. There have been many proposals to increase the freight rates for freight trucks, but they have not been implemented. Several states, such as Nebraska, New Mexico, Oklahoma, Delaware, and Maine, have implemented port-of-entry laws. Although various parties have strongly opposed them, they have remained ineffective. Transportation companies in particular believe that this approach is too illegal. Delaware also implemented this law in the same way because neighboring states implemented it. According to general opinion, this type of legislation is detrimental to the public because it invisibly adds an obstacle between states, like taxation between countries, and it also sees the vehicle license revenue donated by freight truck merchants as exploitation and unfair. Connecticut, Rhode Island, and Delaware have laws regulating the fees and services for freight trucks. The four western states have already changed their laws. The federal government has also promulgated laws to regulate the interstate freight truck industry, which have been in effect since October 1, 1935. However, many people believe that this law is somewhat different from the original intent. There are supporters and opponents.

Overseas Car News Roundup 224

— Yu

Not long after the start of 1936, the US automobile industry also came with new hopes. But how the future will be is still difficult to predict at present, because the instability of the market is similar to the situation two years ago. What the car manufacturers are hoping for now is to get a reasonable return on their investment this year, which would be enough. In 1935, they spent a total of US$100,000,000 on various new components, which cannot be said to be a small amount. The so-called instability of the market has a wide scope. Among them, the development of the retail market is the most concerning for each factory. After the new cars came on the market last winter, the response from all parties was quite good, and the demand was very high. The salespersons of each company also took advantage of the momentum to widely promote sales. As a result, the number of units sold in six weeks was quite impressive. From then on, what the sales scene in the spring of 1936 will be has indeed become an important question. As for the huge amount of money invested by the automobile industry, people in the industry have no worries about it, because this kind of investment is different from consumption, and it is ultimately a permanent asset.

The use of car headlights is extremely important in driving, but drivers often ignore it, which is very strange. According to research by Mr. Philip Cadle, Chief Electrical Engineer of the Desso Automobile Company, after researching 3,200,000 cars, he found that among every ten cars, seven had defects in their headlights. Mr. Cadle also said that 55 percent of car accidents occur at night, and flashing lights and insufficient headlight brightness are major causes of accidents.

Mr. McCade, Manager of Nash Automobile Company, Mr. Brist, Deputy Manager and Director of Sales, and Mr. Connerson, General Sales Manager, conducted a large-scale business inspection at the end of the year and the beginning of spring. All major cities were visited by them. It is said that the impressions gained from this trip were very deep and very pleasant, saying that the future of the automobile industry in 1936 has a vigorous appearance.

The new streamlined Chrysler car has a new type of speedometer. This speedometer, in addition to recording the car's speed per hour in the same way as conventional speedometers, can also let the driver know the engine's speed of rotation. For example, the rotation rate of the third gear and the high-speed driving situation can be seen at a glance.
